                  <form>       
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">جَيِّدٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">جيد</orth>
                  </form>, originally of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَيْعِلٌ</foreign>, (S, Msb,) as the Basrees say, i. e. <foreign lang="ar">جَيْوِدٌ</foreign>, (Msb, TA,) the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> being changed into <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> because of its being meksoor and preceded by <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign>, and the augmentative <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> being then incorporated into it; (TA;) or, as the Koofees say, of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَيْعَلٌ</foreign>, like <foreign lang="ar">عَيْطَلٌ</foreign> &amp;c., because there is found no sound word of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَيْعِلٌ</foreign> except <foreign lang="ar">صَيْقِلٌ</foreign>, a woman's name, and the unsound is accorded to the sound; or, as others say, of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَعِيلٌ</foreign>, [and so I find in one copy of the S,] originally <foreign lang="ar">جَوِيدٌ</foreign>, the kesreh of the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> being, accord. to them, suppressed because difficult of pronunciation, and the quiescent <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> thus coming together, [the latter receives the rejected kesreh, and] the <foreign lang="ar">و</foreign> is changed into <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign> and incorporated into the [augmentative] <foreign lang="ar">ى</foreign>; (Msb;) <hi rend="ital">Good, goodly, approvable,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">excellent; contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">رَدِ ىْ</foreign>; (A, K;) applied to a thing, (S,) or a commodity, an article of household-goods, or the like, (A, Msb,) and a work, or performance: (TA:) pl. <foreign lang="ar">جِيَادٌ</foreign> (S, A, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">جِيَادَاتٌ</foreign>, (K,) the latter a pl. pl., [i. e. pl. of <foreign lang="ar">جِيَادٌ</foreign>,] (TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">جَيَائِدُ</foreign>, (S, K,) with hemz, [and, accord. to some,] contr. to analogy. (S.) [It is also applied to a man, meaning <hi rend="ital">Excellent,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">egregious,</hi> in some quality; sometimes, though very rarely, in a quality that is disapproved.]    </entryFree>2d:T4e7,<entryFree id="n6659" key="أَجْوَدُ" type="main">
